<aside
class="bio">









<p
class="title">about</p>









<p
class="bio">
Despite
a
huge
hit
single
in
the
mid-'70s
(&quot;The
Boys
Are
Back
in
Town&quot;)
and
becoming
a
popular
act
with
hard
rock/heavy
metal
fans,
Thin
Lizzy
are
still,
in
the
pantheon
of
'70s
rock
bands,
underappreciated.
Formed
in
the
late
'60s
by
Irish
singer/so...
</p>









<a
href="/thinlizzynow/bio">read
more</a>








</aside>
